THIS PATCH MAKES PCI_INIT() DETERMINE CLS BY LOOKING AT WHAT FIRMWARE    HAS CONFIGURED.  IT SCANS ALL DEVICES AND IF ALL NON-ZERO VALUES    AGREE, THE VALUE IS USED.
